# Chats in Tech: The POWER Of AI!

**Duration**: PT50M8S
**Views**: 12
**Likes**: 1

**Description**:
Welcome back to our monthly tech check in with 'Chats in Tech' and this time Leo and Justin are discussing the power of AI and how helpful it can be to use a mix of them in the creation of documents, stories and educational material and more. Working through a project in real time!

Join the conversation and share your thoughts in the comments below.
_____________ 

Don't forget to like, comment & subscribe for so you don't miss out!
